   function ez_isclean( data ) {
    if (typeof data === 'undefined') { data = document.URL; }
    var re = /(([^&lt;&gt;()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^&lt;&gt;()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))(@|%2540|%40)((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))/;
    var isClean = !re.test(data);
    return isClean;
}var ez_queue = new Array();
function sort_queue(a, b)
{
  if( a.priority &lt; b.priority ) return -1;
  else if( a.priority == b.priority ) return 0;
  else return 1;  
}
function execute_ez_queue()
{
  ez_queue.sort( sort_queue );

  for( var i in ez_queue )
  {
        if(typeof ez_queue[i].method != "undefined")
        {
            ez_queue[i].method.call( null );
        }
  }
}

var ez_ad_units = new Array();    
function ez_write_tag(d) {
    if(ez_isclean() &amp;&amp; d instanceof Array) {
        try {
            if(isAboveFold(d[1]))
            {
                var sname = d[1].replace(/-/g,"_");
                var slot_name = 'ezslot_'+eval('ezslotn_'+sname);
                var br1 = eval('ezslotb_'+sname);
                eval(slot_name).setTargeting("br1",br1);
            }
        }
        catch(err) {
        }
        ez_ad_units[ez_ad_units.length] = d;
        var ezcmd = "googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-"+d[1]+"-0');});";
        return ezcmd;
    }
    else {
        return "1+1";
    }
}
function isAboveFold(name) {
    var span = document.querySelector('span[id^="div-gpt-ad-'+name+'-"]');
    if (span !== null) {
        var adParent = span.parentNode;
        if (adParent !== null) {
            var adCoords = adParent.getBoundingClientRect();
            var winHeight = "innerHeight" in window ? window.innerHeight : document.documentElement.offsetHeight;
            var winWidth = "innerWidth" in window ? window.innerWidth : document.documentElement.offsetWidth;
            if (adCoords.bottom &lt;= winHeight &amp;&amp; adCoords.right &lt;= winWidth) {
                //adParent.style.border = "13px solid red";
                return true;
            }
        }
    }
    else {
        return false;
    }
    return false;
}
function in_array(needle, haystack) {
    var length = haystack.length;
    for(var i = 0; i &lt; length; i++) {
        if(haystack[i] == needle) return true;
    }
    return false;
}

        function ezoGetCurrentStyles( element ) {

                if(before_span != null)
                {
                    before_span.insertBefore($(element));
                }

                if(ezIgnoreTags.indexOf(element.tagName) == -1)
                {
                    if($(element).hasClass('ezoic-wrapper') == false &amp;&amp; $(element).hasClass('ezoic-no-wrapper') == false)
                    {
                        if($(element).closest('.ezoic-no-wrapper').length &lt; 1 &amp;&amp; $(element).closest('.ezoic-ad').length &lt; 1 &amp;&amp; $(element).closest('.ezo_ad').length &lt; 1 &amp;&amp; $(element).closest('.ezoic-wrapper').length &lt; 1  &amp;&amp; $(element).css('position') != 'fixed' &amp;&amp; $(element).css('position') != 'absolute')
                        {
                            $(element).addClass('ezoic-wrapper');
                            /* this is a kludgy failsafe to prevent the array from going crazy. the checker runs every 200ms, btw. */
                            if (ezo_elements_to_check.length &lt; 100) {
                                ezo_elements_to_check.push(element);
                            }
                            ezo_resize_interval_count=0; //reset interval timer
                            if($(element).hasClass('ez_wrap_ins') == false &amp;&amp; $(element).parent().is('body'))
                            {
                                $(element).wrap("&lt;ins class='ezoic-wrapper ez_wrap_ins'&gt;");
                                $(element).css('max-width','none');
                                //var ezo_style = getComputedStyle(element);
                                var cssText = ezoGetCurrentStyles(element);

                                var rand_class = 'ezo_wrapper_'+Math.floor((Math.random()*100000)+1);

                                var ezoTempStyle = document.createElement('style');
                                /*
                                var cssText = '';
                                if (ezo_style != null) {
                                    cssText = ezo_style.cssText;
                                }
                                */
                                ezoTempStyle.innerHTML = '.'+rand_class+'{'+cssText+'}';
                                document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].insertBefore(ezoTempStyle,document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].firstChild)
                                $(element).addClass('ez_wrap_ins');
                                $(element).addClass(rand_class);
                                $(element).unwrap('ins');
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    });
}
  </script>

          <div class="row" ezoic="wrapper" id="main" style="-webkit-box-sizing: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-origin: padding-box; border-spacing: 0px 0px; box-sizing: border-box; clear: none; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-weight: normal; line-height: 23px; list-style-image: none; list-style-position: outside; list-style-type: disc; text-indent: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; visibility: visible; word-wrap: break-word; zoom: 1; width: 100%;       pwidth: 1;        height: auto; background: transparent; position: static; top: auto; right: auto; left: auto; bottom: auto;    extra-space-allowed: 0; padding-bottom: 54px; margin-top: 36px;margin-bottom: 0px; ">
           <ins class="ezoic-before-el ezoic-bla-0-marker" style="content:none;background-color:transparent;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(0, 128, 0);display:table;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;line-height:23px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;padding-bottom:1px;">

           <div class="c7" ezoic="wrapper" id="primary" style="-webkit-box-sizing: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-origin: padding-box; border-spacing: 0px 0px; box-sizing: border-box; clear: none; float: left; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-weight: normal; line-height: 23px; list-style-image: none; list-style-position: outside; list-style-type: disc; min-height:0px; text-indent: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; visibility: visible; word-wrap: break-word; width: 100%;       pwidth: 1;         height: auto; background: transparent; position: relative; top: auto; right: auto; left: auto; bottom: auto;  padding-right: 12px;padding-left: 12px; ">
            <article class="post-129 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-english-mistakes tag-contractions" id="post-129" style="background-color:transparent;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;float:left;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:131px;-moz-box-sizing:border-box;padding-bottom:11px;">
             <header style="background-color:transparent;">
              <h3 class="post-category" style="background-color:transparent;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:11px;font-weight:300;line-height:18px;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
               <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/category/english-mistakes/" rel="category tag" style="background-color:transparent;color:rgb(102, 102, 102) !important !important;">
                Mistakes + difficulties
               </a>
              </h3>
              <h1 class="entry-title" style="background-color:transparent;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:28px;line-height:33px;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
               Whos vs Whose
              </h1>
              <h2 class="entry-meta" style="background-color:transparent;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:300;line-height:16px;">
              </h2>
             </header>
             <div class="entry-content" style="background-color:transparent;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:131px;padding:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <p style="background-color:transparent;max-width:none;">
               Who knows the difference between
               <i style="background-color:transparent;">
                whos
               </i>
               and
               <i style="background-color:transparent;">
                whose
               </i>
               ? Heres a lesson whose time has come.
              </p>
              <p style="background-color:transparent;max-width:none;">
               <span class="ezoic-ad medrectangle-2" style="display:inline-block;width:300px;min-height:270px;float:left;margin:2px 28px 4px 1px !important;">
                <span class="ezoic-ad" id="div-gpt-ad-elearnenglishlanguage_com-medrectangle-2-0" style="width:300px;position:relative;z-index:501;display:block;">
                 <script data-cfasync="false" style="display:none;" type="text/javascript">
                  eval(ez_write_tag([[300,250],'elearnenglishlanguage_com-medrectangle-2']));
                 </script>
                </span>
               </span>
               <font style="background-color:transparent;color:rgb(153, 0, 153);">
                <b style="background-color:transparent;font-weight:bold;">
                 Whos
                </b>
               </font>
              </p>
              <p style="background-color:transparent;max-width:none;">
               <i style="background-color:transparent;">
                Whos
               </i>
               is a contraction of who is or, less commonly, who has.
              </p>
              <blockquote style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(170, 170, 170);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:10px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;margin-top:5px;margin-right:0px;margin-bottom:1em;margin-left:0px; padding-left: 10px; ">
               <p style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
                Whos watching TV?
               </p>
               <p style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
                Do you know whos going to speak?
               </p>
               <p style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
                Whos ready to go?
               </p>
               <p style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
                Whos in the kitchen?
               </p>
               <p style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
                Whos this?
               </p>
               <p style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
                Whos already eaten?
               </p>
              </blockquote>
              <p style="background-color:transparent;max-width:none;">
               <br/>
               <font style="background-color:transparent;color:rgb(153, 0, 153);">
                <b style="background-color:transparent;font-weight:bold;">
                 Whose
                </b>
               </font>
              </p>
              <p style="background-color:transparent;max-width:none;">
               <i style="background-color:transparent;">
                Whose
               </i>
               is the possessive of who or, somewhat controversially, which.
              </p>
              <blockquote style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(170, 170, 170);border-left-style:solid;border-left-width:10px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;margin-top:5px;margin-right:0px;margin-bottom:1em;margin-left:0px; padding-left: 10px; ">
               <p style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
                Whose book is this?
               </p>
               <p style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
                Do you know whose car this is?
               </p>
               <p style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
                I know a woman whose kids study there.
               </p>
               <p style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
                Whose side are you on?
               </p>
               <p style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:14px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:23px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
                An idea whose time has come.
               </p>
              </blockquote>
              <p style="background-color:transparent;max-width:none;">
              </p>
              <div align="left" style="background-color:transparent;max-width:none;">
               <a href="http://www.anrdoezrs.net/click-1780335-11234463" onmouseout="window.status=' ';return true;" onmouseover="window.status='http://grammarly.com';return true;" style="background-color:transparent;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;color:rgb(61, 151, 194);padding-bottom:1px;" target="_top">
                <br/>
                <img alt="Grammarly - free grammar checker" data-orig-height="250" data-orig-width="300" src="http://www.tqlkg.com/image-1780335-11234463" style="max-width:100%;background-color:transparent;border-bottom-width:0px  !important;border-left-width:0px  !important;border-right-width:0px  !important;border-top-width:0px  !important;width:271px;height:auto;"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <p style="background-color:transparent;max-width:none;">
               <br/>
               <font style="background-color:transparent;color:rgb(153, 0, 153);">
                <b style="background-color:transparent;font-weight:bold;">
                 The Bottom Line
                </b>
               </font>
              </p>
              <p style="background-color:transparent;max-width:none;">
               The trouble here is due to the apostrophe, which on 99% of English words indicates possession, but on this one simply indicates a contraction. If you can replace the word with
               <i style="background-color:transparent;">
                who is
               </i>
               or
               <i style="background-color:transparent;">
                who has
               </i>
               , use
               <i style="background-color:transparent;">
                whos
               </i>
               . If not, use
               <i style="background-color:transparent;">
                whose
               </i>
               .
              </p>
              <p style="background-color:transparent;max-width:none;">
               <span class="ezoic-ad medrectangle-1" style="display:inline-block;width:300px;min-height:270px;float:right;margin:2px 1px 4px 28px !important;">
                <span class="ezoic-ad" id="div-gpt-ad-elearnenglishlanguage_com-medrectangle-1-0" style="width:300px;position:relative;z-index:501;display:block;">

                  eval(ez_write_tag([[300,250],'elearnenglishlanguage_com-medrectangle-1']));
                 </script>
                </span>
               </span>
               <br/>

               </li>
               <li style="background-color:transparent;minimum_paddings:0px 0px 0px 0px;minimum_margins:0px 0px 0px 0px;">

                 <div class="comment-text" style="background-color:transparent; padding: 0px 0px 0px 18px; ">
                  <p style="background-color:transparent;">
                   Youre correct that normally the apostrophe indicates possession, but not in the case of whos where it only indicates a contraction. This is so misused, that when whose is properly placed on a sign or announcement, it is questioned more than if whos is improperly used. Case in point:
                   <br/>
                   Look whose birthday is today! when placed on a sign will invariably garner more questions of misuse than if whos was used.
                  </p>
                 </div>

           <h3 class="widget-title" style="background-color:transparent;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:12px;font-weight:normal;line-height:14px;word-wrap:break-word;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:5px;padding:5px 10px 5px 10px;">
            Mistakes and Difficulties
           </h3>
           <article class="c12 widget-post post-5673 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-english-mistakes" id="post-5673" style="background-color:transparent;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px !important;border-left-width:0px !important;border-right-width:0px !important;border-top-width:0px !important;box-sizing:border-box;clear:both;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);display:block;float:none;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;min-height:1px;position:relative;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:93px;-moz-box-sizing:border-box;margin-bottom:5px;padding-right:10px;padding-bottom:5px;padding-left:10px;">
            <header style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
             <h3 class="post-category" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-transform:uppercase;word-wrap:break-word;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/category/english-mistakes/" rel="category tag" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102) !important !important;font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);">
               Mistakes + difficulties
              </a>
             </h3>
             <h1 class="entry-title" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:20px;font-weight:normal;line-height:25px;word-wrap:break-word;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/english-mistakes/imply-vs-infer/" rel="bookmark" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51) !important !important;font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:20px;font-weight:normal;line-height:25px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(136, 68, 204);" title="Permalink to Imply vs Infer">
               Imply vs Infer
              </a>
             </h1>
             <h2 class="entry-meta" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:300;line-height:15px;word-wrap:break-word;margin-top:2px;">
             </h2>
            </header>
            <div class="entry-content" style="background-color:transparent;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-width:0px;border-right-width:0px;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:70px;-moz-box-sizing:border-box;padding:0px 0px 5px 0px;">
             <p style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;max-width:none;">
              The English verbs
              <i style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
               imply
              </i>
              and
              <i style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
               infer
              </i>
              are often confused by English speakers. Thats not to imply that youre one of them, but if thats how you infer it, go ahead and read this lesson.
             </p>
             <p class="more-link-p" style="box-sizing:border-box;clear:both;float:left;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:42.333333333333px;max-width:none;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a class="more-link" href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/english-mistakes/imply-vs-infer/" style="-webkit-box-shadow:rgb(238, 238, 238) 1px 1px 0px 0px;background-attachment:scroll;background-clip:border-box;background-origin:padding-box;background-position-x:0%;background-position-y:0%;background-repeat:repeat;border-bottom-left-radius:6px;border-bottom-right-radius:6px;border-top-left-radius:6px;border-top-right-radius:6px;box-shadow:rgb(238, 238, 238) 1px 1px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:inline-block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:15px;text-decoration:none;text-shadow:rgb(0, 0, 0) 1px 1px 0px;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(238, 238, 238);margin:1empx 0px 1empx 0px;padding:6px 12px 6px 12px;">
               Read more 
              </a>
             </p>
             <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled" style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:both;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:21px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">

               <h3 class="sd-title" style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);display:inline-block;font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:12px;font-weight:bold;left:auto;line-height:14px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;margin-top:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-bottom:1em;margin-left:0px;">

               </h3>

                   </li>
                  </ul>

            <header style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
             <h3 class="post-category" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-transform:uppercase;word-wrap:break-word;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/category/english-spelling/" rel="category tag" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102) !important !important;font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);">
               English spelling
              </a>
              ,
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/category/english-mistakes/" rel="category tag" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102) !important !important;font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);">
               Mistakes + difficulties
              </a>
             </h3>
             <h1 class="entry-title" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:20px;font-weight:normal;line-height:25px;word-wrap:break-word;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/english-mistakes/stationary-vs-stationery/" rel="bookmark" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51) !important !important;font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:20px;font-weight:normal;line-height:25px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(136, 68, 204);" title="Permalink to Stationary vs Stationery">
               Stationary vs Stationery
              </a>
             </h1>
             <h2 class="entry-meta" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:300;line-height:15px;word-wrap:break-word;margin-top:2px;">
             </h2>
            </header>
            <div class="entry-content" style="background-color:transparent;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-width:0px;border-right-width:0px;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:108px;-moz-box-sizing:border-box;padding:0px 0px 5px 0px;">
             <p style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;max-width:none;">
              The words
              <i style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
               stationary
              </i>
              and
              <i style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
               stationery
              </i>
              are often confused by English speakers due to their similar spelling and pronunciation. If you remain stationary in front of your computer, you can copy this lesson onto your own stationery.
             </p>
             <p class="more-link-p" style="box-sizing:border-box;clear:both;float:left;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:42.333333333333px;max-width:none;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a class="more-link" href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/english-mistakes/stationary-vs-stationery/" style="-webkit-box-shadow:rgb(238, 238, 238) 1px 1px 0px 0px;background-attachment:scroll;background-clip:border-box;background-origin:padding-box;background-position-x:0%;background-position-y:0%;background-repeat:repeat;border-bottom-left-radius:6px;border-bottom-right-radius:6px;border-top-left-radius:6px;border-top-right-radius:6px;box-shadow:rgb(238, 238, 238) 1px 1px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:inline-block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:15px;text-decoration:none;text-shadow:rgb(0, 0, 0) 1px 1px 0px;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(238, 238, 238);margin:1empx 0px 1empx 0px;padding:6px 12px 6px 12px;">
               Read more 
              </a>
             </p>

           <article class="c12 widget-post post-5101 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-english-mistakes" id="post-5101" style="background-color:transparent;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px !important;border-left-width:0px !important;border-right-width:0px !important;border-top-width:0px !important;box-sizing:border-box;clear:both;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);display:block;float:none;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;min-height:1px;position:relative;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:93px;-moz-box-sizing:border-box;margin-bottom:5px;padding-right:10px;padding-bottom:5px;padding-left:10px;">
            <header style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
             <h3 class="post-category" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-transform:uppercase;word-wrap:break-word;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/category/english-mistakes/" rel="category tag" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102) !important !important;font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);">
               Mistakes + difficulties
              </a>
             </h3>
             <h1 class="entry-title" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:20px;font-weight:normal;line-height:25px;word-wrap:break-word;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/english-mistakes/more-than-vs-over/" rel="bookmark" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51) !important !important;font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:20px;font-weight:normal;line-height:25px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(136, 68, 204);" title="Permalink to More than vs Over">
               More than vs Over
              </a>
             </h1>
             <h2 class="entry-meta" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:300;line-height:15px;word-wrap:break-word;margin-top:2px;">
             </h2>
            </header>
            <div class="entry-content" style="background-color:transparent;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-width:0px;border-right-width:0px;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:77px;-moz-box-sizing:border-box;padding:0px 0px 5px 0px;">
             <p style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;max-width:none;">
              Though its no longer official,
              <i style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
               over
              </i>
              is widely considered incorrect when used in front of a number; the correct term is
              <i style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
               more than
              </i>
              . Youll have learned more than you need to know once youve read over this lesson.
             </p>
             <p class="more-link-p" style="box-sizing:border-box;clear:both;float:left;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:42.333333333333px;max-width:none;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a class="more-link" href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/english-mistakes/more-than-vs-over/" style="-webkit-box-shadow:rgb(238, 238, 238) 1px 1px 0px 0px;background-attachment:scroll;background-clip:border-box;background-origin:padding-box;background-position-x:0%;background-position-y:0%;background-repeat:repeat;border-bottom-left-radius:6px;border-bottom-right-radius:6px;border-top-left-radius:6px;border-top-right-radius:6px;box-shadow:rgb(238, 238, 238) 1px 1px 0px 0px;box-sizing:border-box;display:inline-block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:15px;text-decoration:none;text-shadow:rgb(0, 0, 0) 1px 1px 0px;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(238, 238, 238);margin:1empx 0px 1empx 0px;padding:6px 12px 6px 12px;">
               Read more 
              </a>
             </p>
             <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled" style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:both;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:21px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
              <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon-text sd-sharing" style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;left:auto;line-height:21px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;">
               <h3 class="sd-title" style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-top-style:none;border-top-width:0px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);display:inline-block;font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:12px;font-weight:bold;left:auto;line-height:14px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;position:static;right:auto;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;margin-top:0px;margin-right:0px;margin-bottom:1em;margin-left:0px;">
                <ins class="ezoic-before-el ezoic-bla-176-marker" style="-webkit-box-sizing:border-box;background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);background-origin:padding-box;border-bottom-color:rgb(0, 128, 0);border-bottom-style:solid;border-bottom-width:1px;border-left-color:rgb(0, 128, 0);border-left-style:none;border-left-width:0px;border-right-color:rgb(0, 128, 0);border-right-style:none;border-right-width:0px;border-spacing:0px 0px;border-top-color:rgb(221, 221, 221);border-top-style:solid;border-top-width:1px;bottom:auto;box-shadow:none;box-sizing:border-box;clear:none;color:rgb(0, 128, 0);display:block;font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:12px;font-weight:bold;left:auto;line-height:14px;list-style-image:none;list-style-position:outside;list-style-type:disc;min-width:30px;position:static;right:auto;text-decoration:none;text-indent:0px;top:auto;vertical-align:baseline;visibility:visible;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;margin-bottom:1em;">
                </ins>
                Share:
               </h3>

                   </li>
                  </ul>

            <header style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
             <h3 class="post-category" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-transform:uppercase;word-wrap:break-word;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/category/english-spelling/" rel="category tag" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102) !important !important;font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);">
               English spelling
              </a>
              ,
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/category/english-mistakes/" rel="category tag" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102) !important !important;font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);">
               Mistakes + difficulties
              </a>
             </h3>
             <h1 class="entry-title" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:20px;font-weight:normal;line-height:25px;word-wrap:break-word;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/english-mistakes/principal-vs-principle/" rel="bookmark" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51) !important !important;font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:20px;font-weight:normal;line-height:25px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(136, 68, 204);" title="Permalink to Principal vs Principle">
               Principal vs Principle
              </a>
             </h1>
             <h2 class="entry-meta" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:300;line-height:15px;word-wrap:break-word;margin-top:2px;">
             </h2>
            </header>
            <div class="entry-content" style="background-color:transparent;border-bottom-color:rgb(51, 51, 51);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-width:0px;border-right-width:0px;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:77px;-moz-box-sizing:border-box;padding:0px 0px 5px 0px;">
             <p style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;max-width:none;">
              The words
              <i style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
               principal
              </i>
              and
              <i style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
               principle
              </i>
              are often confused by English speakers. Read this lesson to learn the principles of the principal meanings.
             </p>
             <p class="more-link-p" style="box-sizing:border-box;clear:both;float:left;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:42.333333333333px;max-width:none;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">

               Read more 
              </a>
             </p>

            <header style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);display:block;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
             <h3 class="post-category" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-transform:uppercase;word-wrap:break-word;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/category/english-spelling/" rel="category tag" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102) !important !important;font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);">
               English spelling
              </a>
              ,
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/category/english-mistakes/" rel="category tag" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(102, 102, 102) !important !important;font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:10px;font-weight:300;line-height:17px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(102, 102, 102);">
               Mistakes + difficulties
              </a>
             </h3>
             <h1 class="entry-title" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:20px;font-weight:normal;line-height:25px;word-wrap:break-word;margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <a href="http://www.elearnenglishlanguage.com/blog/english-mistakes/advice-vs-advise/" rel="bookmark" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51) !important !important;font-family:'Cantata One', serif;font-size:20px;font-weight:normal;line-height:25px;text-decoration:none;word-wrap:break-word;hover-color:rgb(136, 68, 204);" title="Permalink to Advice vs Advise">
               Advice vs Advise
              </a>
             </h1>
             <h2 class="entry-meta" style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(51, 51, 51);font-family:Lato, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:300;line-height:15px;word-wrap:break-word;margin-top:2px;">
             </h2>
            </header>
            <div class="entry-content" style="background-color:transparent;border-bottom-color:rgb(85, 85, 85);border-bottom-style:none;border-bottom-width:0px;border-left-width:0px;border-right-width:0px;border-top-width:0px;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden;word-wrap:break-word;width:100%;pwidth:1;min-width:62px;-moz-box-sizing:border-box;padding:0px 0px 5px 0px;">
             <p style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;max-width:none;">
              The words
              <i style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
               advice
              </i>
              and
              <i style="background-color:transparent;box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(85, 85, 85);font-family:Arial, sans-serif;font-size:13px;font-weight:normal;line-height:21px;word-wrap:break-word;">
               advise
              </i>
              are often confused in English. I advise you to read through this lesson so you will no longer need advice on this matter.
             </p>

   (function ($) {
    var opt;
    $.fn.printThis = function (options) {
        opt = $.extend({}, $.fn.printThis.defaults, options);
        var $element = this instanceof $ ? this : $(this);

            var strFrameName = "printThis-" + (new Date()).getTime();

            if(window.location.hostname !== document.domain &amp;&amp; navigator.userAgent.match(/msie/i)){
                var iframeSrc = "javascript:document.write(\"&lt;he" + "ad&gt;&lt;scr" + "ipt&gt;document.domain='" + document.domain + "';&lt;/scr" + "ipt&gt;&lt;\/he" + "ad&gt;&lt;bo" + "dy&gt;&lt;\/bo" + "dy&gt;\")";
                var printI= document.createElement('iframe');
                printI.name = "printIframe";
                printI.id = strFrameName;
                printI.className = "MSIE";
                document.body.appendChild(printI);
                printI.src = iframeSrc;

            } else {
                 // other browsers inherit document.domain, and IE works if document.domain is not explicitly set
                var $frame = $("&lt;iframe id='" + strFrameName +"' name='printIframe' /&gt;");
                $frame.appendTo("body");
            }


            var $iframe = $("#" + strFrameName);

            // show frame if in debug mode
            if (!opt.debug) $iframe.css({
                position: "absolute",
                width: "0px",
                height: "0px",
                left: "-600px",
                top: "-600px"
            });


            var $result = null;
            var sep = (window.location.href.indexOf('?') &gt; -1) ? '&amp;' : '?';
            var scriptUrl = window.location.href + sep + "ez_orig=1";
            $.ajax({
               url: scriptUrl,
               type: 'get',
               dataType: 'html',
               async: false,
               success: function(data) {
                   $result = data;
               }
            });


        // $iframe.ready() and $iframe.load were inconsistent between browsers
        setTimeout ( function () {

            var $doc = $iframe.contents();

            //just get the ez_orig and pass it on
            //$doc.find("body").append($result);
            $iframe.get(0).contentWindow.document.open();
            $iframe.get(0).contentWindow.document.write($result);
            $iframe.get(0).contentWindow.document.close();

            var myInterval = setInterval(function () {

                if ($iframe.get(0).contentWindow.document.readyState == 'complete') {

                    clearInterval(myInterval);

                    if($iframe.hasClass("MSIE")){
                        // check if the iframe was created with the ugly hack
                        // and perform another ugly hack out of neccessity
                        window.frames["printIframe"].focus();
                        $doc.find("head").append("&lt;scr" + "ipt&gt; window.print(); &lt;/scr" + "ipt&gt;");
                    } else {
                        // proper method
                        $iframe.get(0).contentWindow.focus();
                        $iframe.get(0).contentWindow.print();
                    }

                    $element.trigger( "done");

                    //remove iframe after print
                    if (!opt.debug) {
                        setTimeout(function () {
                            $iframe.remove();
                        }, 1000);
                    }
                }

            }, opt.printDelay);

        }, 333 );

    };

    // defaults
    $.fn.printThis.defaults = {
        debug: false, // show the iframe for debugging
        importCSS: false, // import parent page css
        printContainer: false, // print outer container/$.selector
        loadCSS: "", // load an additional css file
        pageTitle: "", // add title to print page
        removeInline: false, // remove all inline styles
        printDelay: 500, // variable print delay S. Vance
        header: null // prefix to html
    };

    // $.selector container
    $.fn.outer = function () {
        return $($("&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;").html(this.clone())).html()
    }
})($ezJQuery);

function ezPrintThis()
{
    $ezJQuery('html').printThis();
};/**
 * menu-aim is a jQuery plugin for dropdown menus that can differentiate
 * between a user trying hover over a dropdown item vs trying to navigate into
 * a submenu's contents.
 *
 * menu-aim assumes that you have are using a menu with submenus that expand
 * to the menu's right. It will fire events when the user's mouse enters a new
 * dropdown item *and* when that item is being intentionally hovered over.
 *
 * __________________________
 * | Monkeys  &gt;|   Gorilla  |
 * | Gorillas &gt;|   Content  |
 * | Chimps   &gt;|   Here     |
 * |___________|____________|
 *
 * In the above example, "Gorillas" is selected and its submenu content is
 * being shown on the right. Imagine that the user's cursor is hovering over
 * "Gorillas." When they move their mouse into the "Gorilla Content" area, they
 * may briefly hover over "Chimps." This shouldn't close the "Gorilla Content"
 * area.
 *
 * This problem is normally solved using timeouts and delays. menu-aim tries to
 * solve this by detecting the direction of the user's mouse movement. This can
 * make for quicker transitions when navigating up and down the menu. The
 * experience is hopefully similar to amazon.com/'s "Shop by Department"
 * dropdown.
 *
 * Use like so:
 *
 *      $("#menu").menuAim({
 *          activate: $.noop,  // fired on row activation
 *          deactivate: $.noop  // fired on row deactivation
 *      });
 *
 *  ...to receive events when a menu's row has been purposefully (de)activated.
 *
 * The following options can be passed to menuAim. All functions execute with
 * the relevant row's HTML element as the execution context ('this'):
 *
 *      .menuAim({
 *          // Function to call when a row is purposefully activated. Use this
 *          // to show a submenu's content for the activated row.
 *          activate: function() {},
 *
 *          // Function to call when a row is deactivated.
 *          deactivate: function() {},
 *
 *          // Function to call when mouse enters a menu row. Entering a row
 *          // does not mean the row has been activated, as the user may be
 *          // mousing over to a submenu.
 *          enter: function() {},
 *
 *          // Function to call when mouse exits a menu row.
 *          exit: function() {},
 *
 *          // Selector for identifying which elements in the menu are rows
 *          // that can trigger the above events. Defaults to "&gt; li".
 *          rowSelector: "&gt; li",
 *
 *          // You may have some menu rows that aren't submenus and therefore
 *          // shouldn't ever need to "activate." If so, filter submenu rows w/
 *          // this selector. Defaults to "*" (all elements).
 *          submenuSelector: "*",
 *
 *          // Direction the submenu opens relative to the main menu. Can be
 *          // left, right, above, or below. Defaults to "right".
 *          submenuDirection: "right"
 *      });
 *
 * https://github.com/kamens/jQuery-menu-aim
*/
(function($) {

    $.fn.menuAim = function(opts) {
        // Initialize menu-aim for all elements in jQuery collection
        this.each(function() {
            init.call(this, opts);
        });

        return this;
    };

    function init(opts) {
        var $menu = $(this),
            activeRow = null,
            mouseLocs = [],
            lastDelayLoc = null,
            timeoutId = null,
            options = $.extend({
                rowSelector: "&gt; div",
                submenuSelector: "*",
                submenuDirection: "right",
                tolerance: 75,  // bigger = more forgivey when entering submenu
                enter: $.noop,
                exit: $.noop,
                activate: $.noop,
                deactivate: $.noop,
                exitMenu: $.noop
            }, opts);

        var MOUSE_LOCS_TRACKED = 3,  // number of past mouse locations to track
            DELAY = 300;  // ms delay when user appears to be entering submenu

        /**
         * Keep track of the last few locations of the mouse.
         */
        var mousemoveDocument = function(e) {
                mouseLocs.push({x: e.pageX, y: e.pageY});

                if (mouseLocs.length &gt; MOUSE_LOCS_TRACKED) {
                    mouseLocs.shift();
                }
            };

        /**
         * Cancel possible row activations when leaving the menu entirely
         */
        var mouseleaveMenu = function() {
                if (timeoutId) {
                    clearTimeout(timeoutId);
                }

                // If exitMenu is supplied and returns true, deactivate the
                // currently active row on menu exit.
                if (options.exitMenu(this)) {
                    if (activeRow) {
                        options.deactivate(activeRow);
                    }

                    activeRow = null;
                }
            };

        /**
         * Trigger a possible row activation whenever entering a new row.
         */
        var mouseenterRow = function() {
                if (timeoutId) {
                    // Cancel any previous activation delays
                    clearTimeout(timeoutId);
                }

                options.enter(this);
                possiblyActivate(this);
            },
            mouseleaveRow = function() {
                options.exit(this);
            };

        /*
         * Immediately activate a row if the user clicks on it.
         */
        var clickRow = function() {
                activate(this);
            };

        /**
         * Activate a menu row.
         */
        var activate = function(row) {
                if (row == activeRow) {
                    return;
                }

                if (activeRow) {
                    options.deactivate(activeRow);
                }

                options.activate(row);
                activeRow = row;
            };

        /**
         * Possibly activate a menu row. If mouse movement indicates that we
         * shouldn't activate yet because user may be trying to enter
         * a submenu's content, then delay and check again later.
         */
        var possiblyActivate = function(row) {
                var delay = activationDelay();

                if (delay) {
                    timeoutId = setTimeout(function() {
                        possiblyActivate(row);
                    }, delay);
                } else {
                    activate(row);
                }
            };

        /**
         * Return the amount of time that should be used as a delay before the
         * currently hovered row is activated.
         *
         * Returns 0 if the activation should happen immediately. Otherwise,
         * returns the number of milliseconds that should be delayed before
         * checking again to see if the row should be activated.
         */
        var activationDelay = function() {
                if (!activeRow || !$(activeRow).is(options.submenuSelector)) {
                    // If there is no other submenu row already active, then
                    // go ahead and activate immediately.
                    return 0;
                }

                var offset = $menu.offset(),
                    upperLeft = {
                        x: offset.left,
                        y: offset.top - options.tolerance
                    },
                    upperRight = {
                        x: offset.left + $menu.outerWidth(),
                        y: upperLeft.y
                    },
                    lowerLeft = {
                        x: offset.left,
                        y: offset.top + $menu.outerHeight() + options.tolerance
                    },
                    lowerRight = {
                        x: offset.left + $menu.outerWidth(),
                        y: lowerLeft.y
                    },
                    loc = mouseLocs[mouseLocs.length - 1],
                    prevLoc = mouseLocs[0];

                if (!loc) {
                    return 0;
                }

                if (!prevLoc) {
                    prevLoc = loc;
                }

                if (prevLoc.x &lt; offset.left || prevLoc.x &gt; lowerRight.x ||
                    prevLoc.y &lt; offset.top || prevLoc.y &gt; lowerRight.y) {
                    // If the previous mouse location was outside of the entire
                    // menu's bounds, immediately activate.
                    return 0;
                }

                if (lastDelayLoc &amp;&amp;
                        loc.x == lastDelayLoc.x &amp;&amp; loc.y == lastDelayLoc.y) {
                    // If the mouse hasn't moved since the last time we checked
                    // for activation status, immediately activate.
                    return 0;
                }

                // Detect if the user is moving towards the currently activated
                // submenu.
                //
                // If the mouse is heading relatively clearly towards
                // the submenu's content, we should wait and give the user more
                // time before activating a new row. If the mouse is heading
                // elsewhere, we can immediately activate a new row.
                //
                // We detect this by calculating the slope formed between the
                // current mouse location and the upper/lower right points of
                // the menu. We do the same for the previous mouse location.
                // If the current mouse location's slopes are
                // increasing/decreasing appropriately compared to the
                // previous's, we know the user is moving toward the submenu.
                //
                // Note that since the y-axis increases as the cursor moves
                // down the screen, we are looking for the slope between the
                // cursor and the upper right corner to decrease over time, not
                // increase (somewhat counterintuitively).
                function slope(a, b) {
                    return (b.y - a.y) / (b.x - a.x);
                };

                var decreasingCorner = upperRight,
                    increasingCorner = lowerRight;

                // Our expectations for decreasing or increasing slope values
                // depends on which direction the submenu opens relative to the
                // main menu. By default, if the menu opens on the right, we
                // expect the slope between the cursor and the upper right
                // corner to decrease over time, as explained above. If the
                // submenu opens in a different direction, we change our slope
                // expectations.
                if (options.submenuDirection == "left") {
                    decreasingCorner = lowerLeft;
                    increasingCorner = upperLeft;
                } else if (options.submenuDirection == "below") {
                    decreasingCorner = lowerRight;
                    increasingCorner = lowerLeft;
                } else if (options.submenuDirection == "above") {
                    decreasingCorner = upperLeft;
                    increasingCorner = upperRight;
                }

                var decreasingSlope = slope(loc, decreasingCorner),
                    increasingSlope = slope(loc, increasingCorner),
                    prevDecreasingSlope = slope(prevLoc, decreasingCorner),
                    prevIncreasingSlope = slope(prevLoc, increasingCorner);

                if (decreasingSlope &lt; prevDecreasingSlope &amp;&amp;
                        increasingSlope &gt; prevIncreasingSlope) {
                    // Mouse is moving from previous location towards the
                    // currently activated submenu. Delay before activating a
                    // new menu row, because user may be moving into submenu.
                    lastDelayLoc = loc;
                    return DELAY;
                }

                lastDelayLoc = null;
                return 0;
            };

        /**
         * Hook up initial menu events
         */
        $menu
            .mouseleave(mouseleaveMenu)
            .find(options.rowSelector)
                .mouseenter(mouseenterRow)
                .mouseleave(mouseleaveRow)
                .click(clickRow);

        $(document).mousemove(mousemoveDocument);

    };
})($ezJQuery);$ezJQuery(".ez_mega_parents").menuAim({
            activate: activateMegaMenu,
            deactivate: deactivateMegaMenu
        });

function activateMegaMenu(row)
{
        if(row != null)
        {
          $ezJQuery('.ez_mega_lvl2').hide();
          $ezJQuery('#'+row.id+'_lvl2').show();
          
          $ezJQuery('.ez_mega_lvl1').removeClass('ez_mega_active');
          $ezJQuery('#'+row.id).addClass('ez_mega_active');
        }
}

function deactivateMegaMenu(row)
{
    $ezJQuery('.ez_mega_lvl2').hide();
    $ezJQuery('.ez_mega_lvl1').removeClass('ez_mega_active');
}

var ez_mega_active = '';
function ez_mega_show(selector,active_item_selector,element)
{
    $ezJQuery(ez_mega_active).hide();
    //console.log('show -- '+selector+' active -- '+active_item_selector);
    ez_mega_active = selector;
    $ezJQuery(ez_mega_active).stop(true,true);
    $ezJQuery('.ez_mega').unbind('mouseleave mouseenter');
    
    if(typeof ez_mega_menu_vertical_adjust != 'undefined')
    {
        if(ez_mega_menu_vertical_adjust &amp;&amp; element != undefined)
        {
            $ezJQuery(ez_mega_active).css('top',$ezJQuery(element).closest('ul').position().top);
        }
    }
    
    $ezJQuery(ez_mega_active).show();
    
    $parents = $ezJQuery(ez_mega_active).find('.ez_mega_parents');   
    $parent_height = ($parents.children().last().offset().top + $parents.children().last().outerHeight()) - $parents.offset().top;
    
    if($parent_height &gt; $ezJQuery(ez_mega_active).outerHeight())
    {
        $ezJQuery(ez_mega_active).css('height',$parent_height+'px');
    }
        
    
    activateMegaMenu(document.getElementById($ezJQuery(active_item_selector).attr('id')));
    
    
    $ezJQuery(ez_mega_active).mouseleave(function(){
        //console.log('mouseleave');
        ez_mega_hide();
        
        $ezJQuery(ez_mega_active).mouseenter(function(){
    //console.log('mouseenter');
    ez_mega_show(ez_mega_active);
    });
    
    });
}

function ez_mega_hide()
{
    $ezJQuery(ez_mega_active).delay( 200 ).fadeOut( 500 );
    $ezJQuery('.ez_mega').unbind('mouseleave');
}

        }
    });
}
